<U>Messages<UC><C><L.36.1>
GM Reminder: Free agents are not available after week 17.<L.33.1>
<L.6.1>
<Z>Order of Special Actions <C> I've been asked to clarify the order in which special actions are processed, so here goes. Note<L.31.1>
that it doesn't matter which action (1-5) you write them in, unless it's the same action (so an ACTIVATE action 1 is processed<L.31.1>
before ACTIVATE action 2):-<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Before Games <C> ACTIVATE, PROMOTE, RELEASE (note that players waived are placed temporarily on a "waive squad"), changes to<L.31.1>
game parameters, PLATOON, PINCH, NEWPOS, lineups.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>After Games <C> FANS, STADIUM, MERC, COACH, TRAINER, MINORS, REHAB, Form changes, Stadium changes, ACCEPTS, OFFERS, LISTs, Free<L.31.1>
Agent Bids, Free Agent Signings, Waivers (from the "Waive Squad"), Income and Wages, Form Updates.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Waive Squad <C> Note that one of the wrinkles of the waive squad is that in preseason (and only preseason) you can waive a<L.31.1>
player and still select him the same turn (because he's on the Waive squad when games are processed). It's a minor wrinkle, and I<L.31.1>
can't see it being much use, but it's an option that's there if you want it. Outside of preseason, it doesn't apply.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>9am Deadline <C> Can I remind everyone that orders should be here by 9am (which for postal users means the previous day's<L.31.1>
post). A few people seem to be dribbling in email orders during the morning (or afternoon) so be warned, they will miss the boat.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>2009 Rules - Standings <C> I've set the standings on the 2009 rules to show Minors on odd weeks (1, 3, 5, etc) and Trainers on<L.31.1>
even weeks (2, 4, 6, etc). I can't see you need to see them each week, and there's not space, hence the rotation.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>2009 Rules - Incoming FAs <C> With the new 2009 rules, you may see incoming free agents with silly total form (1000+). I think<L.31.1>
I've stopped the software from creating new ones but there will be a few old ones in the system. If one appears, let me know.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Online Turnsheet <C> The column is now there for MINBATS, and it appears regardless of whether your game has moved up to 2009<L.31.1>
rules or not. You can actually adjust MINBATS under the 2005, but the changes won't appear until you reach 2009 rules, and<L.31.1>
obviously won't come into play until then. All pitchers should start with a default MINBATS of 1 (though I've just added a tweak<L.31.1>
as some had it set to zero, but that should be ironed out over the next few turns).<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Late Email Results <C> If you think results are late, please make sure you wait until the following morning before chasing up<L.31.1>
results. First step is to check out the Latest News at www.pbmsports.com - if I am running late I'll post a notice there. Please<L.31.1>
don't chase me up because you know your mate got his half an hour ago, because whilst most emails are "instant", often they do get<L.31.1>
delayed for a few hours and it does take a while to send them all out (I spread them out to avoid triggering firewalls).<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
Equally however, if it's the next morning and you've not had results, and there's nothing on www.pbmsports.com saying I've had a<L.31.1>
problem, then please chase me up. If it hasn't shown 12 hours later, odds are it won't, and probably some firewall or spam filter<L.31.1>
somewhere has gobbled it (and they do appear to do so without pattern). I'd rather you ended up with two copies than none.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>PDF Reports <C> Emailed game reports are available for all games here. The standard format is a PDF file - Adobe Reader is free<L.1.1>
<P>
<L>
<L.1.1>
to download (see www.pbmsports.com for a link) and you can open your reports with one click of the mouse and you can either view<L.31.1>
them on screen, or print them as you wish. You don't need to worry about formatting or printer drivers. The text format for<L.31.1>
reports is available but I only expect people will want to do so if they use the text file for other purposes (such as exporting<L.31.1>
the listings into software produced yourself). If you've not tried email reports before, try them out - it really is very easy.        <L.31.1>
